 com / 0g314cxuqj There has been increasing opposition among doctors regarding the National Medical Bill (NMC)
 bill ke khilaaf dilli ke ames or safadarganj hospital ke alaava pijiai chandigarh or aligarh muslim uniwarsity (amu)samet desh ke kai sansthaaon main pradarshan kiya gaya
 The demonstration was organized from AIIMS to Parliament House in which more than 10,000 doctors opposed many provisions of the bill
 is bill ke mutabik maujuuda medical council of india kii jagah neshnal medical kamishan body lagu karne kii yojana he
 The bill is also opposed by the Indian Medical Association (IMA)
 deshbhar main doctoron kii ore se baari virodh-pradarshan ke baad sarkaar kii ore se bill ko sansad kii select kamity ke paas bhej diya gaya tha
 The bill provides for the creation of four autonomous boards under the National Medical Bill
 inkaa kaam under graduate or post graduate shiksha ko dekhne ke alaava chikitsa sansthaanon kii manyata or doctoron ke panjikaran kii vyavastha ko dekhnaa hoga
 The commission will have a government-nominated chairman and members, while members on the boards will be selected through a search committee
 yah cabinet sachiv kii nigaraanee main banaai jaaegi
 The panel will consist of 12 former and five selected members
 saath hi is bill main sajhi pravesh pariksha ke saath license pariksha yojit karaane kaa prastaav he
 All graduates must pass the licensure examination to practice
 bill ke jariye sunishchit kiya ja rahaa he ki siten badhaane or post graduate course shuru karne ke liye sansthaanon ko anumati kii jarurat nahin hogi
 It is being said by the government that the purpose of this bill is to bring changes in the medical education sector of the country, besides freeing it from corruption and immoral activities
 duusari ore, ieme kaa kahana he ki isse bade paimaane par chikitsa kaa str giregaa or yah marij kii dekhbhaal or suraksha ke saath khilwaad hoga
 MBBS should remain the standard for practice under modern medical practice
 is bill main ayurveda sahit bhartiya chikitsa paddati ke chikitsakon ko brij course karne ke baad allopathy kii practice kii ijaajat di gai he
 Doctors are also opposing it
 ieme ko bill ke us pravaadhan par bhi aitraaj he jisamen management siton kii fees tay karne kaa adhikaar diya gaya he

 ) smartphone, computer or internet aapaki dincharya main shaamil honge
 You must have talked a lot about security and privacy, but do you remember when was the last time you changed your email or Facebook password? To protect you from dangerous hackers, we tell you some ways by which you can secure your own online presence
 agar aap pehle se in tips par amal karte hai to acchhee baat he, lekin agar pehle aisan nahin kiya to ab vakt aa gaya he
 Safe password - Keep special characters and digits in the password of any account
 caps or small kaa combination bhi rakhen
 Also, change the password at least every six months
 anti virus -premium anti virus yuj karen or use hameshaa apadet rakhen
 Periodically scan your computer and smartphone with it
 apadet -computer or smartphone ke apadats ko kabhi ignor na karen
 Because companies provide security patches through it that protect your system
 kyonki har din nae virus likhe jate hai or puraane oparating system use samaj nahin pate
 Two Step Authentication - Gmail and other online services offer two step authentication features
 agar aapkaa mobile chori yaa clon ho gaya phir bhi koi doosraa aapaki idi ko acces nahin kar saktaa he
 Because OTP comes in every time
 divaais lock -apane smartphone yaa laptop ko har vakt fingerprint scinar yaa pin ke jariye lock rakhen
 Do you know who is the hacker around you and cheat with you? ap instolation -computer or mobile main kisi bhi ap ko install karne se pehle ye dekh len ki wo veryphid publisher kaa he yaa nahin
 Apart from this, also see what information he will get from your smartphone
 router ko sicyor rakhen -agar aapkaa router sicyor nahin he to mumkin he aap 100 fisadi hack ho jaaenge
 Because if the router is hacked then the password can be stolen from the traffic of all the devices connected to it
 isliye isamen majboot password laga kar rakhen or anjaan ko na bataaen
 Email, popup and fake link - Do not open the attachment given in any email which is completely unknown and looks fake
 kyonki havers ke liye sabase aasaan hota he kisi link ke jariye aapke system ko apane control main lenaa
 In the same way, you should also avoid opening any pop up advertisement and fake links that are going viral on social media
 online paison ke lenden main saavdhaanee -onlineshopping ho, kisi ko paise bhejne ho yaa richargekarna ho in sab main aapako saavdhaan rahane kii jarurat he
 Whether it is Internet banking password or credit debit card, before checking their details, the website is secure or not
 website main security kaa digital certificate or URL main padlock kaa iken hona jaruri he
 Public wifi - Do not use any public wifi in the Internet
 kyonki iske jariye aapke smartphone kaa metadata havers aasaani se uda sakate hai
 So before connecting, make sure that it is secure or not
 extra tipswebkaim par tepe laga kar rakhen -chaahe america khufia agency epabai ke diarector hon yaa fasebuk ke siio mark jakarberg apane security ke liye laptop ke webacam par tepe laga kar rakhte hai
